integrate_scandinavia_category = {
	NOR_integrate_scandinavia = {
		icon = generic_form_nation
		visible = {
			NOR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = form_scandinavia_flag }
		}
		available = {
			# Norway
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = integrate_country_norway_required_states_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							region = 11
							region = 191
							state = 1027
						}
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Sweden
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = integrate_country_sweden_required_states_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							region = 10
							region = 192
							state = 124
						}
						state = 1024	#exclude Bornholm
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Denmark / European Mainland
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = integrate_scandinavia_denmark_required_states_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							region = 277
							state = 1024
						}
						state = 998	#only non-Danish part of region 277
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			# Norway
			custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_country_norway_coring_states_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 11
							region = 191
							state = 1027
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = NOR
				}
			}
			# Sweden
			custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_country_sweden_coring_states_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 10
							region = 192
							state = 124
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = NOR
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						145 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes }
					}
					145 = { transfer_state_to = NOR }
				}
			}
			# Denmark / European Mainland
			custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_scandinavia_denmark_coring_states_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 277
							state = 1024
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 998
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = NOR
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
	}

integrate_nordic_league_category = {
	NOR_integrate_nordic_league = {
		icon = generic_form_nation
		visible = {
			NOR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = form_nordic_league_flag }
		}
		available = {
			# Norway
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = integrate_country_norway_required_states_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							region = 11
							region = 191
							state = 1027
						}
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Sweden
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = integrate_country_sweden_required_states_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							region = 10
							region = 192
							state = 124
						}
						state = 1024	#exclude Bornholm
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Denmark
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = integrate_country_denmark_required_states_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							region = 277
							state = 101
							state = 337
							state = 1024
						}
						state = 998	#only non-Danish part of region 277
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Iceland 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = integrate_country_iceland_recuired_states_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							state = 1043
							state = 100
						}
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Finland
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = integrate_country_finland_required_states_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { 
							region = 13	#sorry, but you need Karelia, PetSMIo and Salla too!
							AND = {
								region = 12
								NOT = {
									state = 213	#not Murmansk
								}
							}
							AND = {
								region = 9
								NOT = {
									state = 124	#Aland, not Gotland
								}
							}
						}
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			# Norway
			custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_country_norway_coring_states_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								region = 11
								region = 191
								state = 1027
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = NOR
					}
				}
			}
			# Sweden
			custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_country_sweden_coring_states_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 10
							region = 192
							state = 124
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = NOR
				}
			}
			# Denmark
			custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_country_denmark_coring_states_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 277
							state = 1024
							state = 101
							state = 337
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 998 #You're not getting a free core on Southern Schleswig, it's not Danish
						}	
					}
					transfer_state_to = NOR
				}
			}
			# Iceland
			custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_country_iceland_coring_states_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 1043
							state = 100
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = NOR
				}
			}
			# Finland
			custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_country_finland_coring_states_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 13	#sorry, but you need Karelia, PetSMIo and Salla too!
							AND = {
								region = 12
								NOT = {
									state = 213	#not Murmansk
								}
							}
							AND = {
								region = 9
								NOT = {
									state = 124	#Aland, not Gotland
								}
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = NOR
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = integrate_country_KAR_required_states_tt
						146 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes }
						147 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes }
						213 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes }
						215 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes }
						216 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes }
						722 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes }
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = integrate_country_KAR_coring_states_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					NOR = {
						transfer_state = 146
						transfer_state = 147
						transfer_state = 213
						transfer_state = 215
						transfer_state = 216
						transfer_state = 722
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
	}
